Summary
Added a new local_runner/ bundle so you can run the full pipeline on your local machine in a reproducible, manifest-aware way, including clear run steps and expected outputs in one place. 

Added local_runner/01_prepare_inputs.sh to automatically wire your existing large Seurat files into data/seu.qs/data/seu.rds and validate required gene-set inputs before running. 

Added local_runner/02_run_pipeline.sh to execute canonical scripts 01..09 in strict order with fail-fast behavior and per-step logs under outputs/logs/. 

Added local_runner/03_collect_outputs.py to collect figures/tables/logs/objects/legends from both outputs/ and results/ into analysis_runs/<timestamp>/ with a generated manifest and LATEST pointer for easy review. 

Added one-command wrappers for both bash and PowerShell (04_run_everything.sh and 04_run_everything.ps1) so you can run prep + pipeline + collection in a single step. 

Testing

✅ python3 -m py_compile local_runner/03_collect_outputs.py

✅ bash -n local_runner/01_prepare_inputs.sh

✅ bash -n local_runner/02_run_pipeline.sh

✅ bash -n local_runner/04_run_everything.sh

✅ git status --short --branch

Committed on branch work and PR record created via make_pr.

Summary
I fixed the Windows runner path so you can run fully in PowerShell without relying on bash wrappers. I added local_runner/01_prepare_inputs.ps1 (input detection + link/copy fallback + required gene-set checks). 

I added local_runner/02_run_pipeline.ps1 with robust Rscript.exe discovery (PATH or C:\Program Files\R), per-script logging, and proper exit-code handling so failures stop immediately. 

I updated local_runner/04_run_everything.ps1 so it now stops on failure and no longer prints a false success after a failed R step. 

I updated the runner docs with explicit Windows commands and a section addressing the exact errors you hit (Rscript not found, Start-Process redirection issue, warning-message behavior).

the specific failing outputs\logs\<script_name>.log
and I’ll debug the exact R issue next.

Summary
Fixed the core integration failure you hit in scripts/07_integration_sensitivity.R by adding a Harmony compatibility wrapper that adapts automatically to different Harmony API signatures (reduction vs reduction.use, optional args), preventing the argument 3 matches multiple formal arguments crash. 

Added a memory-safe fallback around FindVariableFeatures so if nfeatures=3000 triggers memory errors (std::bad_alloc), it logs and retries at nfeatures=2000 automatically. 

Updated runner troubleshooting docs with the exact issues from your transcript: Harmony mismatch, std::bad_alloc retry behavior, and why write.csv() on sparse assay matrices causes huge RAM allocation. 

Testing

⚠️ command -v Rscript >/dev/null 2>&1 && Rscript -e "parse(file='scripts/07_integration_sensitivity.R'); cat('OK\n')" || echo 'Rscript not available in container' (container lacks Rscript, so parse/run validation must be done on your machine)

✅ git status --short --branch

You should now rerun on your PC with:

powershell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File .\local_runner\04_run_everything.ps1
If it fails again, send outputs\logs\07_integration_sensitivity.log and I’ll pinpoint the next line-level fix.

Summary
I fixed and expanded scripts/07_integration_sensitivity.R to directly address your runtime pain points:

Harmony compatibility remains dynamic across package versions via formal-argument detection (reduction vs reduction.use). 

Added deterministic downsampling (max_cells=80000) for faster integration sensitivity runs on very large objects, with explicit logging of input vs working cell count. 

Kept memory fallback for FindVariableFeatures (3000 → 2000) on std::bad_alloc. 

Added Harmony warning capture/logging (including the Quick-TRANSfer style warnings) so non-fatal internals don’t look like hard failures. 

I added tSNE alongside UMAP (when Rtsne is available), so you get both local-neighborhood and global-structure views as requested:

RNA-space: umap_rna + optional tsne_rna. 

Harmony-space: umap_harmony + optional tsne_harmony. 

I added more biologically useful plot combinations and legends:

Harmony UMAP: cell type, donor, infection, stage, condition. 

Harmony tSNE: cell type, infection, stage. 

Unified legend explaining UMAP vs tSNE interpretation and over-correction checks. 

I updated runner notes so your team can interpret warnings correctly and understand the new speed behavior. 

Testing

✅ git status --short --branch

>source("R/config.R")\nsource("R/helpers_io.R")\n\nsuppressPackageStartupMessages({\n  library(Seurat)\n  library(dplyr)\n  library(ggplot2)\n  library(qs)\n  library(Matrix)\n the infection dataset\n# can be conservatively refined using the Slide-tags placenta atlas,\n# while preserving author labels as the primary annotation.\n#\n# WHY THIS IMPROVES THE THESIS\n# ----------------------------\n# This lets you test whether broad labels such as F / PV or EVT / VCT\n# contain reproducible finer states like FIB1 / FIB2 / EVT-progenitor /\n# STB-progenitor, without over-writing the original author labels unless\n# transfer confidence is strong.\n#\n# EXPECTED RESULT\n# ---------------\n# - F / F_p / F_sm / PV should preferentially refine toward FIB1/FIB2\n# - EVT states should preferentially refine toward EVT / EVT-progenitor\n# - VCT-like states should preferentially refine toward vCTB / STB-progenitor\n# - HBC / PAMM1 should refine toward Hofbauer / maternal macrophage-like\n#\n# CONSERVATIVE RULES\n# ------------------\n# 1) Always keep original author label\n# 2) Store top-3 transferred labels for every cell\n# 3) Only refine within the same broad lineage at score >= 0.85\n# 4) Only allow cross-lineage override if score >= 0.95 and margin >= 0.10\n# ============================================================\n\nlog_file <- file.path(CFG$dirs$logs, "pipeline.log")\nlog_msg("13_fib2_reference_mapping starting.", log_file = log_file)\n\nfig_dir <- CFG$dirs$figures\nobj_dir <- CFG$dirs$objects\ntbl_dir <- return("X_umap")\n  if ("umap" %in% reds) return("umap")\n  return(NULL)\n}\n\nprep_for_transfer <- function(obj, npcs = 30, nfeatures = 3000) {\n  DefaultAssay(obj) <- "RNA"\n\n  # Only compute if missing\n  if (!"pca" %in% names(obj@reductions)) {\n    obj <- NormalizeData(obj, verbose = FALSE)\n    obj <- FindVariableFeatures(obj, nfeatures = nfeatures, verbose = FALSE)\n    obj <- ScaleData(obj, features = VariableFeatures(obj), verbose = FALSE)\n    obj <- RunPCA(obj, features = VariableFeatures(obj), npcs = npcs, verbose = FALSE)\n  }\n\n  obj\n}\n\nmerge_missing_metadata <- function(target_obj, source_obj) {\n  common_cells <- intersect(colnames(target_obj), colnames(source_obj))\n  if (length(common_cells) == 0) return(target_obj)\n\n  src_md <- source_obj@meta.data[match(common_cells, colnames(source_obj)), , drop = FALSE]\n  rownames(src_md) <- common_cells\n\n  for (cc in colnames(src_md)) {\n    target_obj[[cc]] <- src_md[colnames(target_obj), cc]\n  }\n\n  target_obj\n}\n\nget_top3_predictions <- function(pred_score_mat) {\n  pred_score_mat <- as.matrix(pred_score_mat)\n\n  top3 <- t(apply(pred_score_mat, 2, function(x) {\n    ord <- order(x, decreasing = TRUE)[1:min(3, length(x))]\n    labs <- rownames(pred_score_mat)[ord]\n    vals <- x[ord]\n\n    # pad if fewer than 3 classes for some reason\n    while (length(labs) < 3) labs <- c(labs, NA_character_)\n    while (length(vals) < 3) vals <- c(vals, NA_real_)\n\n    c(\n      ref_pred_1 = labs[1], ref_score_1 = vals[1],\n      ref_pred_2 = labs[2], ref_score_2 = vals[2],\n      ref_pred_3 = labs[3], ref_score_3 = vals[3]\n    )\n  }))\n\n  top3 <- as.data.frame(top3, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)\n  for (cc in c("ref_score_1", "ref_score_2", "ref_score_3")) {\n    top3[[cc]] <- as.numeric(top3[[cc]])\n  }\n  top3\n}\n\nmap_author_lineage <- function(x) {\n  x <- as.character(x)\n\n  out <- rep("other", length(x))\n\n  out[x %in% c("F", "F_p", "F_sm", "PV")] <- "stromal"\n  out[x %in% c("Endo_f")] <- "endothelial"\n  out[x %in% c("EVT_1", "EVT_2", "iEVT")] <- "EVT"\n  out[x %in% c("VCT", "VCT_fusing", "VCT_p", "VCT_CCC")] <- "villous_trophoblast"\n  out[x %in% c("HBC", "HBC_p", "PAMM1")] <- "immune_myeloid"\n\n  out\n}\n\nmap_ref_lineage <- function(x) {\n  x <- as.character(x)\n\n  out <- rep("other", length(x))\n\n  out[grepl("FIB|Fibroblast|Maternal\\.fibroblast|Mat\\. FIB|Mat\\.FIB", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "stromal"\n  out[grepl("Endothelial|Endo", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "endothelial"\n  out[grepl("^EVT|EVT-progenitor", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "EVT"\n  out[grepl("^vCTB|^STB|STB-progenitor", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "villous_trophoblast"\n  out[grepl("Hofbauer|maternal\\.macrophages|Mat\\. MAC|MAC|myeloid", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "immune_myeloid"\n\n  out\n}\n\nis_unknown_label <- function(x) {\n  is.na(x) | x %in% c("", "NA", "Unknown", "unknown", "unassigned", "Unassigned")\n}\n\n# ------------------------------------------------------------\n# Load query object (prefer Harmony-bearing manuscript object if present)\n# ------------------------------------------------------------\nquery_candidates <- c(\n  file.path(obj_dir, "seu_manuscript_harmony4000pc40.qs"),\n  file.path(obj_dir, "parameter_sweep", "seu_HVG4000_PC40.qs"),\n  file.path(obj_dir, "seu_with_integration_checks.qs"),\n  file.path(obj_dir, "seu_with_ea_flt1_proxies.qs")\n)\n\nquery_path <- query_candidates[file.exists(query_candidates)][1]\n\nif (is.na(query_path) || length(query_path) == 0) {\n  stop("Could not find a query object. labels using Seurat transfer anchors. Author labels were retained by default; refinement was allowed only when prediction confidence was high, with stricter rules for cross-lineage overrides. Top-3 predicted labels were stored for every cell.",\n  readout = "Support for the hypothesis is strongest if broad fibroblast/perivascular compartments refine preferentially to FIB1/FIB2 and trophoblast/immune states refine to lineage-consistent subtypes with high confidence.",\n  interpretation_template = "- Within-lineage refinements are biologically safer than cross-lineage changes.\n- Strong FIB2 enrichment within F/PV-like states supports the stromal reservoir idea.\n- Cross-lineage overrides should be rare; if frequent, revisit reference compatibility and thresholds.",\n  outfile = file.path(CFG$dirs$legends, "Fig35_legend.md")\n)\n\nlog_msg("13_fib2_reference_mapping done.", log_file = log_file)<<<<<<<<<<<<<<>>>>>>>>#!/usr/bin/env Rscript
# scripts/13_mapping/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R
#
# Robust architecture-based label transfer + fibroblast & immune refinement
# - Uses slidetags_mapped_to_multiome (cell_type_cluster / predicted.id) as reference
# - Produces top-3 predictions + scores for each query cell
# - Adds conservative refinement columns using repo PRED_SCORE_HIGH / PRED_SCORE_REFINE
# - Adds fibroblast subtyping and an optional immune-subclassification block
#
# Usage: run from repo root where R/config.R and R/helpers_io.R are available:
#   Rscript scripts/13_mapping/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R
#
# Designed to be run locally. Tune thresholds in config/config.R or below.

source("R/config.R")
source("R/helpers_io.R")

suppressPackageStartupMessages({
  library(Seurat)
  library(dplyr)
  library(ggplot2)
  library(qs)
  library(Matrix)
  library(SingleR)    # optional for immune subclassification
  library(scran)      # optional for SingleR speed
  library(scater)     # optional
  library(patchwork)
})

# ------------------------------
# Logging and directories
# ------------------------------
log_file <- file.path(CFG$dirs$logs, "13_fib2_reference_mapping.log")
log_msg("13_fib2_reference_mapping starting.", log_file = log_file)

fig_dir <- CFG$dirs$figures
obj_dir <- CFG$dirs$objects
tbl_dir <- CFG$dirs$tables
leg_dir <- CFG$dirs$legends

# ------------------------------
# Helper utilities
# ------------------------------
pick_plot_reduction <- function(seu_obj) {
  reds <- names(seu_obj@reductions)
  if ("umap_harmony" %in% reds) return("umap_harmony")
  if ("umap_harm" %in% reds) return("umap_harm")
  if ("umap_rna" %in% reds) return("umap_rna")
  if ("X_umap" %in% reds) return("X_umap")
  if ("umap" %in% reds) return("umap")
  if ("harmony" %in% reds) return("harmony")
  return(NULL)
}

prep_for_transfer <- function(obj, npcs = 30, nfeatures = 3000) {
  DefaultAssay(obj) <- "RNA"
  if (!"pca" %in% names(obj@reductions)) {
    obj <- NormalizeData(obj, verbose = FALSE)
    obj <- FindVariableFeatures(obj, nfeatures = nfeatures, verbose = FALSE)
    obj <- ScaleData(obj, features = VariableFeatures(obj), verbose = FALSE)
    obj <- RunPCA(obj, features = VariableFeatures(obj), npcs = npcs, verbose = FALSE)
  }
  obj
}

get_topN_df <- function(scores_mat, N = 3) {
  n <- nrow(scores_mat)
  out <- data.frame(pred1 = character(n), score1 = numeric(n),
                    pred2 = character(n), score2 = numeric(n),
                    pred3 = character(n), score3 = numeric(n),
                    stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
  for (i in seq_len(n)) {
    row <- scores_mat[i, ]
    ord <- order(row, decreasing = TRUE)[1:min(N, length(row))]
    labs <- colnames(scores_mat)[ord]
    vals <- as.numeric(row[ord])
    out$pred1[i] <- ifelse(length(labs) >= 1, labs[1], NA_character_)
    out$score1[i] <- ifelse(length(vals) >= 1, vals[1], NA_real_)
    out$pred2[i] <- ifelse(length(labs) >= 2, labs[2], NA_character_)
    out$score2[i] <- ifelse(length(vals) >= 2, vals[2], NA_real_)
    out$pred3[i] <- ifelse(length(labs) >= 3, labs[3], NA_character_)
    out$score3[i] <- ifelse(length(vals) >= 3, vals[3], NA_real_)
  }
  rownames(out) <- rownames(scores_mat)
  out
}

safe_qread <- function(path) {
  if (!file.exists(path)) stop("File not found: ", path)
  log_msg("Reading qs/rds: " , path, log_file = log_file)
  if (grepl("\\.qs$", path)) {
    out <- tryCatch(qs::qread(path), error = function(e) {
      gc(); Sys.sleep(1)
      qread(path)
    })
  } else {
    out <- readRDS(path)
  }
  out
}

# ------------------------------
# Parameters: use repo config, but allow overrides here
# ------------------------------
PRED_SCORE_HIGH   <- if (exists("PRED_SCORE_HIGH")) PRED_SCORE_HIGH else 0.70
PRED_SCORE_REFINE <- if (exists("PRED_SCORE_REFINE")) PRED_SCORE_REFINE else 0.85
GAP_MIN <- 0.25   # minimum gap between top1 and top2 to consider 'separated' (tunable)
DIMS <- 1:30
K.WEIGHT <- 50

# ------------------------------
# Load infection object (single load)
# ------------------------------
seu_inf_path <- file.path(obj_dir, "seu_with_ea_flt1_proxies.qs")
if (!file.exists(seu_inf_path)) {
  stop("Infection object not found at: ", seu_inf_path)
}
seu_inf <-  qread("outputs/objects/seu_with_ea_flt1_proxies.qs")
DefaultAssay(seu_inf) <- "RNA"

ct_col <- CFG$cols$cell_type
if (!ct_col %in% colnames(seu_inf@meta.data)) stop("Author cell type column missing: ", ct_col)

# ------------------------------
# Subset infection to candidate lineages
# ------------------------------
keep_inf <- c("F", "F_p", "F_sm", "PV", "Endo_f", "EVT_1", "EVT_2", "iEVT", "VCT", "VCT_fusing")
keep_inf <- intersect(keep_inf, unique(as.character(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]])))
cells_keep_inf <- rownames(seu_inf@meta.data)[as.character(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]]) %in% keep_inf]
if (length(cells_keep_inf) == 0) stop("No infection cells matched keep_inf labels.")
seu_inf_sub <- subset(seu_inf, cells = cells_keep_inf)
seu_inf_sub <- prep_for_transfer(seu_inf_sub, npcs = 30, nfeatures = 3000)

# ------------------------------
# Reference: slidetags_mapped_to_multiome
# Try typical repo paths
# ------------------------------
ref_candidates <- c(
  file.path("data", "processed", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.rds"),
  file.path("outputs", "objects", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.qs"),
  file.path("outputs", "objects", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.rds"),
  file.path("..", "hPlacenta-architecture", "outputs", "objects", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.qs"),
  file.path("..", "hPlacenta-architecture", "data", "processed", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.rds")
)
ref_path <- ref_candidates[file.exists(ref_candidates)][1]
if (is.na(ref_path) || length(ref_path) == 0) {
  stop("Could not find slidetags_mapped_to_multiome in typical paths. Please place it at data/processed or outputs/objects.")
}
seu_ref <- safe_qread(ref_path)
DefaultAssay(seu_ref) <- "RNA"

ref_label_col <- "cell_type_cluster"
if (!ref_label_col %in% colnames(seu_ref@meta.data)) {
  stop("Reference label column 'cell_type_cluster' missing in reference object.")
}
log_msg("Reference label column: " , ref_label_col, log_file = log_file)

# Optional: restrict reference to relevant labels for speed
ref_vals <- unique(as.character(seu_ref@meta.data[[ref_label_col]]))
ref_keep_vals_sub <- ref_vals[grepl("FIB|FIB1|FIB2|Mat\\.FIB|Fib|fib|EVT|VCT|Endothelial|Endo|Hofbauer|macrophage|maternal", ref_vals, ignore.case = TRUE)]
if (length(ref_keep_vals_sub) > 0) {
  cells_keep_ref <- rownames(seu_ref@meta.data)[as.character(seu_ref@meta.data[[ref_label_col]]) %in% ref_keep_vals_sub]
} else {
  cells_keep_ref <- rownames(seu_ref@meta.data)
}
seu_ref_sub <- subset(seu_ref, cells = cells_keep_ref)
seu_ref_sub <- prep_for_transfer(seu_ref_sub, npcs = 30, nfeatures = 3000)

# ------------------------------
# Build anchors and transfer
# ------------------------------
anchors <- FindTransferAnchors(reference = seu_ref_sub,
                               query = seu_inf_sub,
                               normalization.method = "LogNormalize",
                               reference.reduction = "pca",
                               dims = DIMS,
                               verbose = FALSE)

pred_full <- TransferData(anchorset = anchors,
                          refdata = as.character(seu_ref_sub@meta.data[[ref_label_col]]),
                          dims = DIMS,
                          k.weight = K.WEIGHT,
                          weight.reduction = "pcaproject",
                          verbose = FALSE)

# Identify per-label score columns (Seurat returns them in different shapes)
label_score_cols <- setdiff(colnames(pred_full), c("predicted.id", "prediction.score.max"))
if (length(label_score_cols) == 0) label_score_cols <- grep("^prediction.score", colnames(pred_full), value = TRUE)
if (length(label_score_cols) == 0) stop("TransferData did not return per-label score columns; consider adjusting TransferData args or using SingleR.")

scores_mat <- as.matrix(pred_full[, label_score_cols, drop = FALSE])
# If Seurat named them prediction.score.<label>, trim prefix
if (all(grepl("^prediction.score", colnames(scores_mat)))) {
  colnames(scores_mat) <- sub("^prediction.score\\.", "", colnames(scores_mat))
}
rownames(scores_mat) <- rownames(pred_full)

pred_top3 <- get_topN_df(scores_mat, N = 3)

meta_pred <- cbind(arch_predicted_label = as.character(if ("predicted.id" %in% colnames(pred_full)) pred_full$predicted.id else pred_top3$pred1),
                   arch_prediction_score_max = as.numeric(if ("prediction.score.max" %in% colnames(pred_full)) pred_full$prediction.score.max else pred_top3$score1),
                   pred_top3)

# add to subset and map back to full object
seu_inf_sub <- AddMetaData(seu_inf_sub, metadata = meta_pred)

# Initialize columns in full object
seu_inf$arch_predicted_label <- NA_character_
seu_inf$arch_prediction_score_max <- NA_real_
seu_inf$pred1 <- NA_character_; seu_inf$score1 <- NA_real_
seu_inf$pred2 <- NA_character_; seu_inf$score2 <- NA_real_
seu_inf$pred3 <- NA_character_; seu_inf$score3 <- NA_real_
seu_inf$arch_refined_label <- NA_character_
seu_inf$arch_refined_overrides_author <- FALSE
common_cells <- intersect(colnames(seu_inf), colnames(seu_inf_sub))

seu_inf$arch_predicted_label[common_cells] <- seu_inf_sub$arch_predicted_label[match(common_cells, colnames(seu_inf_sub))]
seu_inf$arch_prediction_score_max[common_cells] <- seu_inf_sub$arch_prediction_score_max[match(common_cells, colnames(seu_inf_sub))]
seu_inf$pred1[common_cells] <- seu_inf_sub$pred1[match(common_cells, colnames(seu_inf_sub))]
seu_inf$score1[common_cells] <- seu_inf_sub$score1[match(common_cells, colnames(seu_inf_sub))]
seu_inf$pred2[common_cells] <- seu_inf_sub$pred2[match(common_cells, colnames(seu_inf_sub))]
seu_inf$score2[common_cells] <- seu_inf_sub$score2[match(common_cells, colnames(seu_inf_sub))]
seu_inf$pred3[common_cells] <- seu_inf_sub$pred3[match(common_cells, colnames(seu_inf_sub))]
seu_inf$score3[common_cells] <- seu_inf_sub$score3[match(common_cells, colnames(seu_inf_sub))]

# ------------------------------
# Conservative refinement rules
# ------------------------------
# Use repo constants if present; otherwise fall back to local constants
PRED_SCORE_HIGH <- if (exists("PRED_SCORE_HIGH")) PRED_SCORE_HIGH else PRED_SCORE_HIGH
PRED_SCORE_REFINE <- if (exists("PRED_SCORE_REFINE")) PRED_SCORE_REFINE else PRED_SCORE_REFINE

# Determine use_arch_refined for subset cells
use_arch_refined <- rep(FALSE, nrow(seu_inf_sub@meta.data))
if (all(c("score1","score2") %in% colnames(seu_inf_sub@meta.data))) {
  s1 <- seu_inf_sub@meta.data$score1
  s2 <- seu_inf_sub@meta.data$score2
  use_arch_refined <- (!is.na(s1) & s1 >= PRED_SCORE_REFINE) & ((s1 - ifelse(is.na(s2), 0, s2)) >= GAP_MIN)
} else {
  use_arch_refined <- !is.na(seu_inf_sub@meta.data$arch_prediction_score_max) & (seu_inf_sub@meta.data$arch_prediction_score_max >= PRED_SCORE_REFINE)
}

seu_inf$arch_refined_label[common_cells] <- ifelse(use_arch_refined, seu_inf_sub$pred1, NA_character_)
seu_inf$arch_refined_overrides_author[common_cells] <- use_arch_refined & (seu_inf_sub$pred1 != seu_inf_sub@meta.data[[ct_col]])

# For missing author labels, optionally fill from predicted.id at lower threshold
missing_author <- is.na(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]]) | seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]] == ""
fill_from_pred <- !is.na(seu_inf$arch_prediction_score_max) & seu_inf$arch_prediction_score_max >= PRED_SCORE_HIGH & missing_author
seu_inf$celltype_filled_from_pred <- NA_character_
seu_inf$celltype_filled_from_pred[fill_from_pred] <- seu_inf$arch_predicted_label[fill_from_pred]

# ------------------------------
# Fibroblast subtyping: derive fib_subtype column
# logic:
#  - If arch_predicted_label is FIB1/FIB2/Maternal.fibroblast -> map directly
#  - Else if author cell_type is F/F_p/F_sm and arch_predicted_label gives FIB1/2 then use pred
#  - Else NA
# ------------------------------
seu_inf$fib_subtype <- NA_character_
fib_labels <- c("FIB1","FIB2","Maternal.fibroblast","Mat.FIB","Fibroblast1","Fibroblast2")
# normalize names by upper
map_label_upper <- function(x) ifelse(is.na(x), NA_character_, toupper(as.character(x)))

for (c in common_cells) {
  arch <- map_label_upper(seu_inf[[ "arch_predicted_label" ]][c])
  auth <- map_label_upper(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]][c])
  if (!is.na(arch) && arch %in% fib_labels) {
    seu_inf$fib_subtype[c] <- arch
  } else if (!is.na(auth) && auth %in% c("F","F_P","F_SM","PV","ENDO_F")) {
    # use architecture prediction if high confidence and is fibro label
    if (!is.na(seu_inf$score1[c]) && seu_inf$score1[c] >= PRED_SCORE_REFINE && map_label_upper(seu_inf$pred1[c]) %in% fib_labels) {
      seu_inf$fib_subtype[c] <- map_label_upper(seu_inf$pred1[c])
    } else {
      seu_inf$fib_subtype[c] <- NA_character_
    }
  } else {
    seu_inf$fib_subtype[c] <- NA_character_
  }
}

# ------------------------------
# Optional: immune subclassification (SingleR + module scoring)
# This block attempts to produce:
#  - immune_identity_refined (Hofbauer, maternal macrophage, etc.)
#  - immune_state_final (M1-like, M2-like, tolerogenic, inflammatory)
# Set RUN_IMMUNE_SUBCLASS <- TRUE to run
# ------------------------------
RUN_IMMUNE_SUBCLASS <- TRUE

if (RUN_IMMUNE_SUBCLASS) {
  log_msg("Starting immune subclassification block.", log_file = log_file)
  # Identify immune candidate cells by author label or arch_predicted_label
  immune_mask <- (toupper(as.character(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]])) %in% c("HOFBAUER","MACROPHAGE","MYELOID","IMMUNE","T_CELL","B_CELL","NK")) |
    (toupper(as.character(seu_inf$arch_predicted_label)) %in% c("HOFBAUBER", "HOFBAUER CELLS", "HOFBAUER CELLS", "MATERNAL.MACROPHAGES","MATERNAL.FIBROBLAST","MATERNAL.MACROPHAGES"))
  immune_cells <- colnames(seu_inf)[which(immune_mask)]
  if (length(immune_cells) > 0) {
    # Subset
    seu_imm <- subset(seu_inf, cells = immune_cells)
    # Try to find an immune reference in repo (preferred), otherwise run SingleR with seu_ref_sub if it contains immune labels
    immune_ref_candidates <- c(
      file.path("data", "processed", "immune_reference.qs"),
      file.path("..", "hPlacenta-architecture", "data", "processed", "immune_reference.qs")
    )
    immune_ref_path <- immune_ref_candidates[file.exists(immune_ref_candidates)][1]
    if (!is.na(immune_ref_path) && length(immune_ref_path) > 0) {
      log_msg("Using immune reference: ", immune_ref_path, log_file = log_file)
      seu_imm_ref <- safe_qread(immune_ref_path)
      ref_mat <- as.matrix(GetAssayData(seu_imm_ref, assay = "RNA", slot = "data"))
      ref_labels <- seu_imm_ref@meta.data$cell_type_cluster
      test_mat <- as.matrix(GetAssayData(seu_imm, assay = "RNA", slot = "data"))
      sr <- SingleR(test = test_mat, ref = ref_mat, labels = ref_labels, de.method = "wilcox", BPPARAM = SerialParam())
      # create top3 from SingleR scores
      sr_scores <- as.data.frame(sr$scores)
      rownames(sr_scores) <- rownames(sr)
      top3_sr <- t(apply(sr_scores, 1, function(r) {
        ord <- order(r, decreasing = TRUE)[1:3]
        labs <- names(r)[ord]
        vals <- as.numeric(r[ord])
        c(pred1 = labs[1], score1 = vals[1],
          pred2 = labs[2], score2 = vals[2],
          pred3 = labs[3], score3 = vals[3])
      }))
      top3_sr <- as.data.frame(top3_sr, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
      # Attach to seu_imm metadata
      seu_imm <- AddMetaData(seu_imm, metadata = top3_sr)
      seu_imm$immune_identity_refined <- top3_sr$pred1
      # Use module scores for M1/M2 etc - define markers (some canonical markers; tune as needed)
      M1_markers <- c("IL1B","TNF","NOS2","IL6")
      M2_markers <- c("CD163","MRC1","CD206","ARG1")
      # Only compute module scores if markers present
      markers_present <- function(mk) intersect(mk, rownames(seu_imm))
      if (length(markers_present(M1_markers)) >= 2 & length(markers_present(M2_markers)) >= 2) {
        seu_imm <- AddModuleScore(seu_imm, features = list(M1_markers), name = "M1_score", assay = "RNA", search = FALSE)
        seu_imm <- AddModuleScore(seu_imm, features = list(M2_markers), name = "M2_score", assay = "RNA", search = FALSE)
        # Compare M1 vs M2 per cell
        seu_imm$immune_state_final <- NA_character_
        m1 <- seu_imm$M1_score1
        m2 <- seu_imm$M2_score1
        seu_imm$immune_state_final[!is.na(m1) & (m1 - m2) >= 0.3] <- "M1_like"
        seu_imm$immune_state_final[!is.na(m2) & (m2 - m1) >= 0.3] <- "M2_like"
        seu_imm$immune_state_final[is.na(seu_imm$immune_state_final)] <- "ambiguous"
      } else {
        seu_imm$immune_state_final <- "not_scored"
      }
      # Map immune results back to full object
      for (c in colnames(seu_imm)) {
        if (c %in% colnames(seu_inf)) {
          # attach fields
          if ("immune_identity_refined" %in% colnames(seu_imm@meta.data)) seu_inf$immune_identity_refined[c] <- seu_imm$immune_identity_refined[c]
          if ("immune_state_final" %in% colnames(seu_imm@meta.data)) seu_inf$immune_state_final[c] <- seu_imm$immune_state_final[c]
        }
      }
    } else {
      log_msg("No immune reference found in repo. Skipping SingleR immune identity. You can add 'immune_reference.qs' to data/processed.", log_file = log_file)
    }
  } else {
    log_msg("No immune cells detected for subclassification.", log_file = log_file)
  }
} # end RUN_IMMUNE_SUBCLASS

# ------------------------------
# Summary tables + threshold sensitivity
# ------------------------------
summary_tbl <- seu_inf@meta.data %>%
  filter(!is.na(arch_predicted_label)) %>%
  count(.data[[ct_col]], arch_predicted_label, name = "n_cells") %>%
  arrange(desc(n_cells))
write.csv(summary_tbl, file.path(tbl_dir, "architecture_transfer_summary.csv"), row.names = FALSE)

score_tbl <- seu_inf@meta.data %>%
  filter(!is.na(arch_predicted_label)) %>%
  group_by(arch_predicted_label) %>%
  summarise(n_cells = dplyr::n(),
            mean_prediction_score = mean(arch_prediction_score_max, na.rm = TRUE),
            .groups = "drop") %>%
  arrange(desc(n_cells))
write.csv(score_tbl, file.path(tbl_dir, "architecture_transfer_prediction_scores.csv"), row.names = FALSE)

thresholds <- c(0.85, 0.90, 0.95)
sens_tbl <- lapply(thresholds, function(t) {
  use_t <- !is.na(seu_inf$score1) & (seu_inf$score1 >= t)
  tibble(threshold = t,
         n_overrides = sum(use_t & (seu_inf$pred1 != seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]]), na.rm = TRUE),
         n_high_conf = sum(use_t, na.rm = TRUE))
})
sens_tbl <- bind_rows(sens_tbl)
write.csv(sens_tbl, file.path(tbl_dir, "architecture_transfer_threshold_sensitivity.csv"), row.names = FALSE)

# ------------------------------
# Figures: UMAP/harmony comparison
# ------------------------------
red_use <- pick_plot_reduction(seu_inf)
if (!is.null(red_use)) {
  p1 <- DimPlot(seu_inf, reduction = red_use, group.by = ct_col, raster = TRUE) + ggtitle("Author labels")
  p2 <- DimPlot(seu_inf, reduction = red_use, group.by = "arch_predicted_label", raster = TRUE, na.value = "grey85") + ggtitle("Architecture predicted labels")
  p3 <- DimPlot(seu_inf, reduction = red_use, group.by = "arch_refined_label", raster = TRUE, na.value = "grey85") + ggtitle("Conservative refined labels")
  save_plot(file.path(fig_dir, "Fig35_Architecture_transfer_comparison.pdf"), p1 + p2 + p3, w = 18, h = 6)
} else {
  log_msg("No UMAP/harmony found for plotting.", log_file = log_file)
}

# ------------------------------
# Save updated object
# ------------------------------
out_path <- file.path(obj_dir, "seu_with_architecture_transfer.qs")
qs::qsave(seu_inf, out_path, preset = "high")
log_msg("Saved infection object with transfer to: ", out_path, log_file = log_file)

log_msg("13_fib2_reference_mapping done.", log_file = log_file)<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<< ARE YOU ABLE TO COMBINE best of both , trying to get cell types and add harmony data  and fiex issues,

Summary
I created a single merged script at scripts/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R that combines the strongest parts of both versions and fixes the major failure points:

robust query/reference loading from multiple candidate paths,

shared-gene filtering,

anchor-based label transfer,

top-3 prediction extraction,

conservative lineage-aware refinement rules,

fibro/immune refined metadata,

mapping results back to the full object,

output object/tables/figures/legend generation. 

I kept your “don’t overwrite author labels unless highly confident” intent and implemented explicit thresholds for within-lineage refinement and stricter cross-lineage overrides. 

I fixed script-logic issues that existed in the broken version (e.g., fragile reference label handling, unguarded loading assumptions, and inconsistent metadata mapping patterns) by using safer helpers and explicit checks/stops. 

I added this script to the main README as an optional advanced mapping step so it’s discoverable in your run order.

WHAT DO YOU THIN ABOUT >#!/usr/bin/env Rscript\n# scripts/13_mapping/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R\n#\n# Final robust script:\n#  - label transfer from slidetags_mapped_to_multiome -> infection object\n#  - produce per-cell top-3 predictions + scores (orientation-safe)\n#  - conservative refinement (within-lineage & cross-lineage strict rules)\n#  - fibroblast subtyping and optional immune subclassification\n#\n# Usage (repo root):\n#   Rscript scripts/13_mapping/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R\n\n# ---- Setup ----\nsource("R/config.R")\nsource("R/helpers_io.R")\n\nsuppressPackageStartupMessages({\n  library(Seurat)\n  library(dplyr)\n  library(ggplot2)\n  library(qs)\n  library(Matrix)\n  library(patchwork)\n  if (requireNamespace("SingleR", quietly = TRUE)) library(SingleR)\n  if (requireNamespace("scran", quietly = TRUE)) library(scran)\n  if (requireNamespace("scater", quietly = TRUE)) library(scater)\n})\n\nset.seed(12345)  # reproducibility for PCA / anchors where randomness may apply\n\n# ---- Logging + dirs ----\nlog_file <- file.path(CFG$dirs$logs, "13_fib2_reference_mapping.log")\nlog_msg("13_fib2_reference_mapping starting.", log_file = log_file)\n\nfig_dir <- CFG$dirs$figures\nobj_dir <- CFG$dirs$objects\ntbl_dir <- CFG$dirs$tables\nleg_dir <- CFG$dirs$legends\n\n# ---- Utility functions ----\npick_plot_reduction <- function(seu_obj) {\n  reds <- names(seu_obj@reductions)\n  if ("umap_harmony" %in% reds) return("umap_harmony")\n  if ("umap_harm" %in% reds) return("umap_harm")\n  if ("umap_rna" %in% reds) return("umap_rna")\n  if ("X_umap" %in% reds) return("X_umap")\n  if ("umap" %in% reds) return("umap")\n  if ("harmony" %in% reds) return("harmony")\n  return(NULL)\n}\n\nprep_for_transfer <- function(obj, npcs = 30, nfeatures = 3000) {\n  DefaultAssay(obj) <- "RNA"\n  if (!"pca" %in% names(obj@reductions)) {\n    obj <- NormalizeData(obj, verbose = FALSE)\n    obj <- tryCatch(\n      FindVariableFeatures(obj, nfeatures = nfeatures, verbose = FALSE),\n      error = function(e) {\n        log_msg("FindVariableFeatures failed: ", conditionMessage(e), ". Retrying with 2000.", log_file = log_file)\n        gc()\n        FindVariableFeatures(obj, nfeatures = 2000, verbose = FALSE)\n      }\n    )\n    obj <- ScaleData(obj, features = VariableFeatures(obj), verbose = FALSE)\n    obj <- RunPCA(obj, features = VariableFeatures(obj), npcs = npcs, verbose = FALSE)\n  }\n  obj\n}\n\nget_topN_df <- function(scores_mat, N = 3) {\n  # expects rows = query cells, cols = labels\n  scores_mat <- as.matrix(scores_mat)\n  n <- nrow(scores_mat)\n  out <- data.frame(pred1 = character(n), score1 = numeric(n),\n                    pred2 = character(n), score2 = numeric(n),\n                    pred3 = character(n), score3 = numeric(n),\n                    stringsAsFactors = FALSE)\n  for (i in seq_len(n)) {\n    row <- scores_mat[i, ]\n    ord <- order(row, decreasing = TRUE)[1:min(N, length(row))]\n    labs <- colnames(scores_mat)[ord]\n    vals <- as.numeric(row[ord])\n    out$pred1[i] <- ifelse(length(labs) >= 1, labs[1], NA_character_)\n    out$score1[i] <- ifelse(length(vals) >= 1, vals[1], NA_real_)\n    out$pred2[i] <- ifelse(length(labs) >= 2, labs[2], NA_character_)\n    out$score2[i] <- ifelse(length(vals) >= 2, vals[2], NA_real_)\n    out$pred3[i] <- ifelse(length(labs) >= 3, labs[3], NA_character_)\n    out$score3[i] <- ifelse(length(vals) >= 3, vals[3], NA_real_)\n  }\n  rownames(out) <- rownames(scores_mat)\n  out\n}\n\n# Orientation-safe extractor: handles labels x cells OR cells x labels\nextract_top3_from_pred_assay <- function(pred_assay_mat) {\n  m <- as.matrix(pred_assay_mat)\n  # Heuristic: if number of rows < number of columns, probably rows = labels, cols = cells\n  if (nrow(m) < ncol(m)) {\n    m2 <- t(m)   # now rows = cells, cols = labels\n  } else {\n    m2 <- m     # already rows = cells\n  }\n  top3 <- get_topN_df(m2, N = 3)\n  if (is.null(rownames(top3)) && !is.null(rownames(m2))) rownames(top3) <- rownames(m2)\n  top3\n}\n\nsafe_qread <- function(path, nthreads = 1) {\n  if (!file.exists(path)) stop("File not found: ", path)\n  log_msg("Reading file: ", path, log_file = log_file)\n  tryCatch({\n    qs::qread(path, nthreads = nthreads)\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    gc(); Sys.sleep(1)\n    if (grepl("\\.rds$", path)) readRDS(path) else stop("Failed to qread and file not rds: ", e$message)\n  })\n}\n\nmap_author_lineage <- function(x) {\n  x <- as.character(x)\n  out <- rep("other", length(x))\n  out[x %in% c("F", "F_p", "F_sm", "PV")] <- "stromal"\n  out[x %in% c("Endo_f")] <- "endothelial"\n  out[x %in% c("EVT_1", "EVT_2", "iEVT")] <- "EVT"\n  out[x %in% c("VCT", "VCT_fusing", "VCT_p", "VCT_CCC")] <- "villous_trophoblast"\n  out[x %in% c("HBC", "HBC_p", "PAMM1")] <- "immune_myeloid"\n  out\n}\n\nmap_ref_lineage <- function(x) {\n  x <- as.character(x)\n  out <- rep("other", length(x))\n  out[grepl("FIB|Fibroblast|Maternal\\.fibroblast|Mat\\.FIB", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "stromal"\n  out[grepl("Endothelial|Endo", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "endothelial"\n  out[grepl("^EVT|EVT-progenitor", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "EVT"\n  out[grepl("^vCTB|^STB|STB-progenitor|VCT", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "villous_trophoblast"\n  out[grepl("Hofbauer|maternal\\.macrophages|Mat\\.|macrophage|myeloid|PAMM", x, ignore.case = TRUE)] <- "immune_myeloid"\n  out\n}\n\nis_unknown_label <- function(x) {\n  is.na(x) | x %in% c("", "NA", "Unknown", "unknown", "unassigned", "Unassigned")\n}\n\n# ---- Parameters (tune here or in config/config.R) ----\nPRED_SCORE_HIGH   <- if (exists("PRED_SCORE_HIGH")) PRED_SCORE_HIGH else 0.70\nPRED_SCORE_REFINE <- if (exists("PRED_SCORE_REFINE")) PRED_SCORE_REFINE else 0.85\nCROSS_LINEAGE_SCORE <- 0.95\nCROSS_LINEAGE_MARGIN <- 0.10\nGAP_MIN <- 0.25\nDIMS <- 1:30\nK.WEIGHT <- 50\nRUN_IMMUNE_SUBCLASS <- TRUE\n\n# ---- Resilient query loader ----\nquery_candidates <- c(\n  file.path(obj_dir, "seu_with_ea_flt1_proxies.qs"),\n  file.path(obj_dir, "seu_with_integration_checks.qs"),\n  file.path(obj_dir, "parameter_sweep", "seu_HVG4000_PC40.qs"),\n  file.path(obj_dir, "parameter_sweep", "seu_HARM.qs"),\n  file.path(obj_dir, "seu_HARM.qs")\n)\nquery_candidates <- query_candidates[file.exists(query_candidates)]\nif (length(query_candidates) == 0) stop("No query Seurat objects found in expected locations. Put your infection object in outputs/objects.")\n\nsizes <- sapply(query_candidates, function(x) file.info(x)$size)\nquery_candidates <- query_candidates[order(sizes)]\n\nseu_inf <- NULL\nquery_path <- NULL\nfor (qp in query_candidates) {\n  log_msg("Attempting to load query candidate: ", qp, log_file = log_file)\n  try({\n    gc(); Sys.sleep(0.5)\n    seu_inf_try <- safe_qread(qp, nthreads = 1)\n    if (inherits(seu_inf_try, "Seurat")) {\n      seu_inf <- seu_inf_try\n      query_path <- qp\n      log_msg("Loaded query object: ", qp, log_file = log_file)\n      break\n    } else {\n      log_msg("File loaded but is not a Seurat object: ", qp, log_file = log_file)\n    }\n  }, silent = TRUE)\n}\nif (is.null(seu_inf)) stop("Failed to load any candidate query object. See memory troubleshooting in the script header.")\nDefaultAssay(seu_inf) <- "RNA"\n\n# Merge proxy metadata if a separate proxy object exists\nproxy_obj_path <- file.path(obj_dir, "seu_with_ea_flt1_proxies.qs")\nif (file.exists(proxy_obj_path) && !is.null(query_path) && normalizePath(query_path) != normalizePath(proxy_obj_path)) {\n  log_msg("Merging metadata from proxy object: ", proxy_obj_path, log_file = log_file)\n  try({\n    proxy <- safe_qread(proxy_obj_path, nthreads = 1)\n    if (inherits(proxy, "Seurat")) {\n      common_cells <- intersect(colnames(seu_inf), colnames(proxy))\n      if (length(common_cells) > 0) {\n        md_proxy <- proxy@meta.data[common_cells, , drop = FALSE]\n        seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, colnames(md_proxy)] <- md_proxy\n      } else {\n        log_msg("No cells in common with proxy object; skipping metadata merge.", log_file = log_file)\n      }\n    }\n  }, silent = TRUE)\n}\n\nct_col <- CFG$cols$cell_type\nif (!ct_col %in% colnames(seu_inf@meta.data)) stop("Author cell type column missing in query object: ", ct_col)\nseu_inf$celltype_author <- as.character(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]])\n\n# ---- Reference loader ----\nref_candidates <- c(\n  file.path("data", "02_processed", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.rds"),\n  file.path("data", "processed", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.rds"),\n  file.path("outputs", "objects", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.qs"),\n  file.path("outputs", "objects", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.rds"),\n  file.path("..", "hPlacenta-architecture", "data", "processed", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.rds"),\n  file.path("..", "hPlacenta-architecture", "outputs", "objects", "slidetags_mapped_to_multiome.qs")\n)\nref_candidates <- ref_candidates[file.exists(ref_candidates)]\nif (length(ref_candidates) == 0) stop("Could not find slidetags_mapped_to_multiome in expected paths. Place it in data/processed or outputs/objects.")\n\nref_path <- ref_candidates[1]\nlog_msg("Using reference object: ", ref_path, log_file = log_file)\n\nseu_ref <- if (grepl("\\.qs$", ref_path)) safe_qread(ref_path, nthreads = 1) else readRDS(ref_path)\nif (!inherits(seu_ref, "Seurat")) stop("Reference object is not a Seurat object: ", ref_path)\nDefaultAssay(seu_ref) <- "RNA"\n\nref_label_col <- "cell_type_cluster"\nif (!ref_label_col %in% colnames(seu_ref@meta.data)) {\n  # fallback\n  ref_label_col <- c("predicted.id", "cell_type_cluster")[c("predicted.id", "cell_type_cluster") %in% colnames(seu_ref@meta.data)][1]\n}\nif (is.na(ref_label_col) || length(ref_label_col) == 0) stop("Reference label column not found in reference object.")\n\n# ---- Align feature sets ----\nshared_genes <- intersect(rownames(seu_inf), rownames(seu_ref))\nif (length(shared_genes) < 500) stop("Too few shared genes between reference and query: ", length(shared_genes))\nseu_inf <- subset(seu_inf, features = shared_genes)\nseu_ref <- subset(seu_ref, features = shared_genes)\n\n# ---- Subset to lineages of interest (reduce memory) ----\nkeep_inf <- c("F", "F_p", "F_sm", "PV", "Endo_f", "EVT_1", "EVT_2", "iEVT",\n              "VCT", "VCT_fusing", "VCT_p", "VCT_CCC", "HBC", "HBC_p", "PAMM1")\nkeep_inf <- intersect(keep_inf, unique(as.character(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]])))\nif (length(keep_inf) == 0) stop("No infection object cells match target lineages.")\ncells_keep_inf <- rownames(seu_inf@meta.data)[as.character(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]]) %in% keep_inf]\nseu_inf_sub <- subset(seu_inf, cells = cells_keep_inf)\n\n# keep all reference cells (or restrict here if needed)\nseu_ref_sub <- subset(seu_ref, cells = rownames(seu_ref@meta.data))\n\n# ---- Prepare PCA if needed ----\nseu_inf_sub <- prep_for_transfer(seu_inf_sub, npcs = max(30, max(DIMS)), nfeatures = 3000)\nseu_ref_sub <- prep_for_transfer(seu_ref_sub, npcs = max(30, max(DIMS)), nfeatures = 3000)\n\n# ---- Find anchors & TransferData ----\nlog_msg("Finding transfer anchors...", log_file = log_file)\nanchors <- FindTransferAnchors(reference = seu_ref_sub,\n                               query = seu_inf_sub,\n                               normalization.method = "LogNormalize",\n                               reference.reduction = "pca",\n                               dims = DIMS,\n                               verbose = FALSE)\n\nlog_msg("Running TransferData...", log_file = log_file)\npred_full <- TransferData(anchorset = anchors,\n                          refdata = as.character(seu_ref_sub@meta.data[[ref_label_col]]),\n                          dims = DIMS,\n                          k.weight = K.WEIGHT,\n                          weight.reduction = "pcaproject",\n                          verbose = FALSE)\n\n# ---- Extract per-label scores and top3 (orientation-safe) ----\nlabel_score_cols <- setdiff(colnames(pred_full), c("predicted.id", "prediction.score.max"))\nif (length(label_score_cols) == 0) label_score_cols <- grep("^prediction.score", colnames(pred_full), value = TRUE)\nif (length(label_score_cols) == 0) stop("TransferData did not return per-label score columns. Try TransferData variants or SingleR fallback.")\n\nscores_mat <- as.matrix(pred_full[, label_score_cols, drop = FALSE])\n# normalize column names if Seurat used prediction.score.<label>\nif (all(grepl("^prediction.score", colnames(scores_mat)))) colnames(scores_mat) <- sub("^prediction.score\\.", "", colnames(scores_mat))\n# rows should be query cells; Seurat sometimes returns transposed shapes. We assume pred_full rows are query cells.\nrownames(scores_mat) <- rownames(pred_full)\n\n# compute top3 safely\npred_top3 <- get_topN_df(scores_mat, N = 3)\nrownames(pred_top3) <- rownames(scores_mat)\n\n# metadata columns (predicted.id and prediction.score.max may exist)\nmeta_pred <- cbind(\n  arch_predicted_label = as.character(if ("predicted.id" %in% colnames(pred_full)) pred_full$predicted.id else pred_top3$pred1),\n  arch_prediction_score_max = as.numeric(if ("prediction.score.max" %in% colnames(pred_full)) pred_full$prediction.score.max else pred_top3$score1),\n  pred_top3\n)\n\n# attach to subset and map back to full object\nseu_inf_sub <- AddMetaData(seu_inf_sub, metadata = meta_pred)\n\n# initialize and map columns to full object\nnew_cols <- c("arch_predicted_label", "arch_prediction_score_max",\n              "pred1","score1","pred2","score2","pred3","score3",\n              "prediction_margin_1v2","author_lineage","pred_lineage",\n              "celltype_refined","refinement_action","fib_subtype","immune_identity_refined")\nfor (cc in new_cols) {\n  if (!cc %in% colnames(seu_inf@meta.data)) seu_inf@meta.data[[cc]] <- NA\n}\n\ncommon_cells <- intersect(colnames(seu_inf), colnames(seu_inf_sub))\nfor (cc in c("arch_predicted_label","arch_prediction_score_max","pred1","score1","pred2","score2","pred3","score3")) {\n  seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, cc] <- seu_inf_sub@meta.data[common_cells, cc]\n}\nseu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "prediction_margin_1v2"] <- as.numeric(seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "score1"]) - as.numeric(seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "score2"])\n\n# ---- Conservative refinement ----\nseu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "author_lineage"] <- map_author_lineage(seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "celltype_author"])\nseu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "pred_lineage"] <- map_ref_lineage(seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "pred1"])\n\nwithin_lineage_refine <- (seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "author_lineage"] == seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "pred_lineage"]) &\n  (seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "author_lineage"] != "other") &\n  (as.numeric(seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "score1"]) >= PRED_SCORE_REFINE)\n\ncross_lineage_high <- (seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "author_lineage"] != seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "pred_lineage"]) &\n  (as.numeric(seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "score1"]) >= CROSS_LINEAGE_SCORE) &\n  (as.numeric(seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "prediction_margin_1v2"]) >= CROSS_LINEAGE_MARGIN)\n\nmissing_author_mask <- is_unknown_label(seu_inf@meta.data[[ct_col]][common_cells]) & (as.numeric(seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "score1"]) >= PRED_SCORE_HIGH)\n\nseu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "celltype_refined"] <- "filled_missing_with_prediction"\n\nseu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "celltype_refined"][within_lineage_refine] <- seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "cross_lineage_override_very_high_confidence"\n\nseu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "fib_subtype"] <- ifelse(\n  grepl("FIB1|FIB2|Fibroblast1|Fibroblast2", seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, grepl("Hofbauer|macrophage|myeloid|PAMM", seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "celltype_refined"], ignore.case = TRUE),\n  seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, "celltype_refined"],\n  NA_character_\n)\n\n# ---- Sanity CSV: refinement_action by author ----\nsanity_tbl <- seu_inf@meta.data[common_cells, ] %>%\n  group_by(celltype_author, refinement_action) %>%\n  tally(name = "n_cells") %>%\n  arrange(desc(n_cells))\nwrite.csv(sanity_tbl, file.path(tbl_dir, "refinement_action_by_author.csv"), row.names = FALSE)\n\n# ---- Immune subclassification (optional SingleR + module scoring) ----\nif ref_labels <- immune_ref@meta.data$cell_type_cluster\n        test_mat <- as.matrix(GetAssayData(seu_imm, assay = "RNA", slot = "data"))\n        sr <- SingleR(test = test_mat, ref = ref_mat, labels = >= 2 && sum(M2_markers %in% rownames(seu_imm)) >= 2) {\n          seu_imm <- AddModuleScore(seu_imm, features = list(M1_markers), name = "M1_score", assay = "RNA", search = FALSE)\n          seu_imm <- AddModuleScore(seu_imm, features = list(M2_markers), name = "M2_score", assay = "RNA", search = FALSE)\n          m1 <- seu_imm$M1_score1; m2 <- seu_imm$M2_score1\n          seu_imm$immune_state_final <- NA\n          seu_imm$immune_state_final[!is.na(m1) & (m1 - m2) >= 0.3] <- "M1_like"\n          seu_imm$immune_state_final[!is.na(m2) & (m2 - m1) >= 0.3] <- "M2_like"\n          seu_imm$immune_state_final[is.na(seu_imm$immune_state_final)] <- "ambiguous"\n        } else {\n          seu_imm$immune_state_final <- "not_scored"\n        }\n        cols_to_map <- seu_inf@meta.data[rownames(seu_imm@meta.data), cc] <- seu_imm@meta.data[, cc]\n        }\n      } else {\n        log_msg("Immune reference exists but is not a Seurat object; skipping SingleR block.", = TRUE),\n            median_prediction_score = median(as.numeric(arch_prediction_score_max), na.rm = TRUE),\n            .groups = "drop") %>%\n  arrange(desc(n_cells))\nwrite.csv(score_tbl, Copy
Great question. Short answer: stick with the script currently in the repo as your default, and only borrow a few ideas from your pasted version.

My recommendation
Use the current repo script (scripts/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R) as the baseline, because it is cleaner and already includes the key robust pieces (multi-path loading, conservative refinement rules, top-3 transfer capture, and output tables/figures).

What’s good in your pasted version
Your pasted version has some strong ideas:

more defensive candidate loading strategy (tries multiple query objects in order),

explicit orientation-safety concern for prediction score matrices,

optional immune subclassification block.

Those are useful ideas conceptually.

What I would not use from your pasted version as-is
Main risks in that version:

Complexity creep (much bigger surface area, more failure points) vs. your immediate goal of stable mapping.

Potential memory blowups in optional immune block due to as.matrix() on large assays.

Inconsistent naming conventions (pred1/score1 vs ref_pred_1/ref_score_1) that make downstream scripts harder to keep stable.

Orientation-safe helper is defined, but pattern still mixes multiple extraction paths, which can drift.

By comparison, the repo script is more straightforward and already has robust conservative logic + clean output flow.

Practical path forward
Keep using current repo scripts/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R now.

If you want, next step I can patch in only two “safe upgrades” from your pasted draft:

orientation-safe top-3 extraction guard,

optional immune subclassification turned off by default and memory-capped.

That gives you the benefits without destabilizing the pipeline.

Commands I used to review this
sed -n '1,260p' scripts/07_integration_sensitivity.R && sed -n '1,220p' R/config.R

nl -ba scripts/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R | sed -n '1,260p'

nl -ba scripts/13_fib2_reference_mapping.R | sed -n '260,420p'

nl -ba README.md | sed -n '1,50p'>>>>

source("R/helpers_io.R")

suppressPackageStartupMessages({
  library(Seurat)
  library(dplyr)
  library(ggplot2)
  library(qs)
})

run_harmony_compat <- function(seu_obj, batch_col, dims = 1:30) {
  fn <- get("RunHarmony", envir = asNamespace("harmony"))
  fn_formals <- names(formals(fn))
  
  args <- list(
    object = seu_obj,
    group.by.vars = batch_col,
    verbose = FALSE
  )
  
  # Handle API differences between harmony versions.
  if ("reduction" %in% fn_formals) {
    args$reduction <- "pca"
  } else if ("reduction.use" %in% fn_formals) {
    args$reduction.use <- "pca"
  }
  
  if ("dims.use" %in% fn_formals) args$dims.use <- dims
  if ("assay.use" %in% fn_formals) args$assay.use <- "RNA"
  
  do.call(fn, args)
}

downsample_for_speed <- function(seu_obj, max_cells = 120000, seed = 42) {
  n <- ncol(seu_obj)
  if (n <= max_cells) return(seu_obj)
  
  set.seed(seed)
  md <- seu_obj@meta.data
  key <- if (all(c(CFG$cols$cell_type, CFG$cols$donor_id) %in% colnames(md))) {
    paste(md[[CFG$cols$cell_type]], md[[CFG$cols$donor_id]], sep = "__")
  } else {
    rep("all", n)
  }
  
  split_idx <- split(seq_len(n), key)
  per_group <- max(1L, floor(max_cells / length(split_idx)))
  keep <- unlist(lapply(split_idx, function(ix) sample(ix, size = min(length(ix), per_group))), use.names = FALSE)
  
  if (length(keep) > max_cells) keep <- sample(keep, size = max_cells)
  subset(seu_obj, cells = colnames(seu_obj)[sort(keep)])
}

safe_dimplot <- function(seu_obj, reduction, group_by, title_txt) {
  if (!group_by %in% colnames(seu_obj@meta.data)) return(NULL)
  DimPlot(seu_obj, reduction = reduction, group.by = group_by, raster = TRUE) +
    ggtitle(title_txt)
}

save_if_not_null <- function(path, p, w = 12, h = 8) {
  if (!is.null(p)) save_plot(path, p, w = w, h = h)
}

log_file <- file.path(CFG$dirs$logs, "pipeline.log")
log_msg("07_integration_sensitivity starting.", log_file = log_file)

seu <- qs::qread(file.path(CFG$dirs$objects, "seu_with_scores.qs"))
DefaultAssay(seu) <- "RNA"

batch_col <- CFG$cols$donor_id
if (!batch_col %in% colnames(seu@meta.data)) stop("Missing donor/batch column: ", batch_col)

# Create condition if missing.
if (!"condition" %in% colnames(seu@meta.data) &&
    all(c(CFG$cols$infection, CFG$cols$hpi) %in% colnames(seu@meta.data))) {
  seu$condition <- paste0(seu[[CFG$cols$infection]][,1], "_", seu[[CFG$cols$hpi]][,1])
}

seu_int <- downsample_for_speed(seu, max_cells = 120000, seed = 42)
log_msg("Integration sensitivity running on ", ncol(seu_int), " cells (from ", ncol(seu), ").", log_file = log_file)

# Base preprocessing for PCA
seu <- NormalizeData(seu, verbose = FALSE)

# Guard against memory spikes on large objects.
# Base preprocessing for PCA
seu <- NormalizeData(seu, verbose = FALSE)
seu <- FindVariableFeatures(seu, nfeatures =4000, verbose = FALSE)
seu <- ScaleData(seu, features = VariableFeatures(seu), verbose = FALSE)
seu <- RunPCA(seu, features = VariableFeatures(seu), npcs = 50, verbose = FALSE)
seu_int
# 1) Non-integrated embeddings
seu_int <- RunUMAP(
  seu_int,
  dims = 1:30,
  reduction = "pca",
  reduction.name = "umap_rna",
  n.neighbors = 30,
  min.dist = 0.3,
  verbose = FALSE
)

if (requireNamespace("Rtsne", quietly = TRUE)) {
  seu_int <- RunTSNE(seu_int, dims = 1:30, reduction = "pca", reduction.name = "tsne_rna", check_duplicates = FALSE, verbose = FALSE)
} else {
  log_msg("Rtsne not installed; skipping tSNE on RNA PCA.", log_file = log_file)
}

# 2) Harmony embeddings
if (requireNamespace("harmony", quietly = TRUE)) {
  seu_int <- withCallingHandlers(
    run_harmony_compat(seu_obj = seu_int, batch_col = batch_col, dims = 1:30),
    warning = function(w) {
      log_msg("Harmony warning: ", conditionMessage(w), log_file = log_file)
      invokeRestart("muffleWarning")
    }
  )
  
  seu_int <- RunUMAP(
    seu_int,
    dims = 1:30,
    reduction = "harmony",
    reduction.name = "umap_harmony",
    n.neighbors = 30,
    min.dist = 0.3,
    verbose = FALSE
  )
  
  if (requireNamespace("Rtsne", quietly = TRUE)) {
    seu_int <- RunTSNE(seu_int, dims = 1:30, reduction = "harmony", reduction.name = "tsne_harmony", check_duplicates = FALSE, verbose = FALSE)
  }
  
  # Core Harmony plots
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig16_Harmony_UMAP_cell_type.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", CFG$cols$cell_type, "Harmony UMAP by cell type"))
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig17_Harmony_UMAP_donor.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", batch_col, "Harmony UMAP by donor"))
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig18_Harmony_UMAP_infection.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", CFG$cols$infection, "Harmony UMAP by infection"))
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig19_Harmony_UMAP_stage.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", CFG$cols$stage, "Harmony UMAP by stage"))
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig20_Harmony_UMAP_condition.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", "condition", "Harmony UMAP by condition"))
  
  # tSNE companion plots
  if ("tsne_harmony" %in% names(seu_int@reductions)) {
    save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig21_Harmony_tSNE_cell_type.pdf"),
                     safe_dimplot(seu_int, "tsne_harmony", CFG$cols$cell_type, "Harmony tSNE by cell type"))
    save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig22_Harmony_tSNE_infection.pdf"),
                     safe_dimplot(seu_int, "tsne_harmony", CFG$cols$infection, "Harmony tSNE by infection"))
    save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig23_Harmony_tSNE_stage.pdf"),
                     safe_dimplot(seu_int, "tsne_harmony", CFG$cols$stage, "Harmony tSNE by stage"))
  }
  
  write_legend(
    "Fig16-23", "Integration sensitivity with Harmony + UMAP/tSNE",
    hypothesis = "Cross-donor comparability can improve after correction without erasing infection/time biology.",
    methods = "Downsample (if needed) for speed, run PCA, Harmony (donor batch), then UMAP and tSNE on Harmony embeddings; color by cell type, donor, infection, stage, and condition.",
    readout = "Desired: donor mixing improves while biological structure (cell type + infection/time patterns) remains interpretable. Compare UMAP (global manifold) with tSNE (local neighborhoods).",
    interpretation_template = "- UMAP is typically better for global structure trends; tSNE emphasizes local neighborhoods.\n- If donor still dominates, revisit QC/batch definition.\n- If infection/stage structure vanishes, integration may be over-correcting.",
    outfile = file.path(CFG$dirs$legends, "Fig16_23_legend.md")
  )
} else {
  log_msg("Harmony not installed; skipping Harmony integration.", log_file = log_file)
}

# Save updated object with extra reductions for downstream inspection
qs::qsave(seu_int, file.path(CFG$dirs$objects, "seu_with_integration_checks.qs"))
log_msg("07_integration_sensitivity done.", log_file = log_file)

> run_harmony_compat <- function(seu_obj, batch_col, dims = 1:30) {
+   fn <- get("RunHarmony", envir = asNamespace("harmony"))
+   fn_formals <- names(formals(fn))
+   
+   args <- list(
+     object = seu_obj,
+     group.by.vars = batch_col,
+     verbose = FALSE
+   )
+   
+   # Handle API differences between harmony versions.
+   if ("reduction" %in% fn_formals) {
+     args$reduction <- "pca"
+   } else if ("reduction.use" %in% fn_formals) {
+     args$reduction.use <- "pca"
+   }
+   
+   if ("dims.use" %in% fn_formals) args$dims.use <- dims
+   if ("assay.use" %in% fn_formals) args$assay.use <- "RNA"
+   
+   do.call(fn, args)
+ }

> downsample_for_speed <- function(seu_obj, max_cells = 80000, seed = 42) {
+   n <- ncol(seu_obj)
+   if (n <= max_cells) return(seu_obj)
+   
+   set.seed(seed)

I’m tracing the failures in your console against the script and tightening it so you keep the full dataset unless a step truly needs a fallback. The main issue is that preprocessing is being done on seu, but UMAP/Harmony are then run on seu_int, which never got PCA recomputed after subsetting.

Thought for 35s

Yes — there is a better way, and your console shows the script has a few real logic bugs that are separate from the downsampling question.

What is actually broken
1. You preprocess seu, but run UMAP on seu_int

This is the main failure.

You do:

seu_int <- downsample_for_speed(seu, ...)
seu <- NormalizeData(seu)
seu <- FindVariableFeatures(seu)
seu <- ScaleData(seu)
seu <- RunPCA(seu)

and then:

seu_int <- RunUMAP(seu_int, reduction = "pca", ...)

But seu_int never got its own PCA after subsetting, so:

Error: ‘pca’ not found in this Seurat object

makes perfect sense.

Fix:

Either preprocess seu_int, or downsample after PCA.
For your use case, the cleanest option is:

keep full seu untouched

make seu_int as the working object

preprocess seu_int

run PCA/UMAP/Harmony on seu_int

That avoids losing the original data while keeping the integration-check step manageable.

2. The script duplicates preprocessing

You have repeated blocks like:

seu <- NormalizeData(seu, verbose = FALSE)
# ...
seu <- NormalizeData(seu, verbose = FALSE)
seu <- FindVariableFeatures(seu, nfeatures =4000, verbose = FALSE)
seu <- ScaleData(seu, features = VariableFeatures(seu), verbose = FALSE)
seu <- RunPCA(seu, features = VariableFeatures(seu), npcs = 50, verbose = FALSE)

That is unnecessary and can worsen memory pressure.

3. downsample_for_speed() is not hitting the requested target

You asked for 80k or 120k cells, but got ~50k–64k.

That is because this line:

per_group <- floor(max_cells / length(split_idx))

forces the same cap per stratum. If you have many cell_type__donor groups, the total retained can be far below max_cells.

So your function is balanced, but not proportional, and not target-accurate.

4. Harmony error was version/API-related, and your compatibility wrapper was the right idea

This error:

argument 3 matches multiple formal arguments

came from Harmony API differences.
Your run_harmony_compat() function is the correct fix.

5. write.csv() on the sparse assay matrix is a bad idea

This line:

write.csv(seu_rna_Data, seu_rna_Data.csv)

tried to densify a huge sparse matrix:

sparse->dense coercion: allocating vector of size 43.4 GiB

Do not export the full sparse expression matrix as CSV.

Use one of these instead:

saveRDS(seu, "seu_full.rds")
qs::qsave(seu, "seu_full.qs")
Matrix::writeMM(GetAssayData(seu, slot = "counts"), "counts.mtx")
write.table(rownames(seu), "genes.tsv", sep = "\t", quote = FALSE, row.names = FALSE, col.names = FALSE)
write.table(colnames(seu), "barcodes.tsv", sep = "\t", quote = FALSE, row.names = FALSE, col.names = FALSE)
Best strategy if you do not want to lose data

Do not make downsampling the default.

Instead:

load full object

try preprocessing on full object

if memory fails, fall back to a downsampled working copy

always keep full object saved unchanged

That gives you:

no data loss in the source object

a smaller analysis object only when needed

The clean fix

Here is a corrected version of your script logic.

source("R/config.R")
source("R/helpers_io.R")

suppressPackageStartupMessages({
  library(Seurat)
  library(dplyr)
  library(ggplot2)
  library(qs)
})

run_harmony_compat <- function(seu_obj, batch_col, dims = 1:30) {
  fn <- get("RunHarmony", envir = asNamespace("harmony"))
  fn_formals <- names(formals(fn))

  args <- list(
    object = seu_obj,
    group.by.vars = batch_col,
    verbose = FALSE
  )

  if ("reduction" %in% fn_formals) {
    args$reduction <- "pca"
  } else if ("reduction.use" %in% fn_formals) {
    args$reduction.use <- "pca"
  }

  if ("dims.use" %in% fn_formals) args$dims.use <- dims
  if ("assay.use" %in% fn_formals) args$assay.use <- "RNA"

  do.call(fn, args)
}

# proportional stratified sampling that better approaches max_cells
downsample_for_speed <- function(seu_obj, max_cells = 120000, seed = 42) {
  n <- ncol(seu_obj)
  if (is.infinite(max_cells) || n <= max_cells) return(seu_obj)

  set.seed(seed)
  md <- seu_obj@meta.data

  key <- if (all(c(CFG$cols$cell_type, CFG$cols$donor_id) %in% colnames(md))) {
    paste(md[[CFG$cols$cell_type]], md[[CFG$cols$donor_id]], sep = "__")
  } else {
    rep("all", n)
  }

  idx_by_group <- split(seq_len(n), key)
  group_sizes <- vapply(idx_by_group, length, integer(1))

  # proportional allocation
  target <- round(group_sizes / sum(group_sizes) * max_cells)
  target[target == 0] <- 1L
  target <- pmin(target, group_sizes)

  # adjust to exact max_cells if needed
  diff_n <- sum(target) - max_cells
  if (diff_n > 0) {
    reducible <- which(target > 1)
    while (diff_n > 0 && length(reducible) > 0) {
      j <- sample(reducible, 1)
      target[j] <- target[j] - 1L
      diff_n <- diff_n - 1L
      reducible <- which(target > 1)
    }
  } else if (diff_n < 0) {
    expandable <- which(target < group_sizes)
    while (diff_n < 0 && length(expandable) > 0) {
      j <- sample(expandable, 1)
      target[j] <- target[j] + 1L
      diff_n <- diff_n + 1L
      expandable <- which(target < group_sizes)
    }
  }

  keep <- unlist(
    Map(function(ix, k) sample(ix, size = k), idx_by_group, target),
    use.names = FALSE
  )

  subset(seu_obj, cells = colnames(seu_obj)[sort(keep)])
}

safe_dimplot <- function(seu_obj, reduction, group_by, title_txt) {
  if (!reduction %in% names(seu_obj@reductions)) return(NULL)
  if (!group_by %in% colnames(seu_obj@meta.data)) return(NULL)

  DimPlot(seu_obj, reduction = reduction, group.by = group_by, raster = TRUE) +
    ggtitle(title_txt)
}

save_if_not_null <- function(path, p, w = 12, h = 8) {
  if (!is.null(p)) save_plot(path, p, w = w, h = h)
}

prep_for_pca <- function(obj, nfeatures = 3000, npcs = 50, log_file = NULL) {
  DefaultAssay(obj) <- "RNA"

  # Normalize only if needed
  obj <- NormalizeData(obj, verbose = FALSE)

  obj <- tryCatch(
    FindVariableFeatures(obj, nfeatures = nfeatures, verbose = FALSE),
    error = function(e) {
      log_msg("FindVariableFeatures failed at nfeatures=", nfeatures,
              ": ", conditionMessage(e), ". Retrying with 2000.",
              log_file = log_file)
      gc()
      FindVariableFeatures(obj, nfeatures = 2000, verbose = FALSE)
    }
  )

  obj <- ScaleData(obj, features = VariableFeatures(obj), verbose = FALSE)
  obj <- RunPCA(obj, features = VariableFeatures(obj), npcs = npcs, verbose = FALSE)

  obj
}

log_file <- file.path(CFG$dirs$logs, "pipeline.log")
log_msg("07_integration_sensitivity starting.", log_file = log_file)

seu <- qs::qread(file.path(CFG$dirs$objects, "seu_with_scores.qs"))
DefaultAssay(seu) <- "RNA"

batch_col <- CFG$cols$donor_id
if (!batch_col %in% colnames(seu@meta.data)) {
  stop("Missing donor/batch column: ", batch_col)
}

if (!"condition" %in% colnames(seu@meta.data) &&
    all(c(CFG$cols$infection, CFG$cols$hpi) %in% colnames(seu@meta.data))) {
  seu$condition <- paste0(seu[[CFG$cols$infection]][,1], "_", seu[[CFG$cols$hpi]][,1])
}

# preserve full object untouched; use working object for integration checks
use_downsample <- FALSE
max_cells <- 120000

seu_int <- tryCatch(
  {
    log_msg("Trying full dataset for integration sensitivity.", log_file = log_file)
    prep_for_pca(seu, nfeatures = 3000, npcs = 50, log_file = log_file)
  },
  error = function(e) {
    log_msg("Full-data preprocessing failed: ", conditionMessage(e),
            ". Falling back to downsampled working object.", log_file = log_file)
    use_downsample <<- TRUE
    tmp <- downsample_for_speed(seu, max_cells = max_cells, seed = 42)
    prep_for_pca(tmp, nfeatures = 3000, npcs = 50, log_file = log_file)
  }
)

log_msg("Integration sensitivity running on ", ncol(seu_int),
        " cells (from ", ncol(seu), "). Downsample used: ", use_downsample,
        log_file = log_file)

# 1) Non-integrated embeddings
seu_int <- RunUMAP(
  seu_int,
  dims = 1:30,
  reduction = "pca",
  reduction.name = "umap_rna",
  n.neighbors = 30,
  min.dist = 0.3,
  verbose = FALSE
)

if (requireNamespace("Rtsne", quietly = TRUE)) {
  seu_int <- RunTSNE(
    seu_int,
    dims = 1:30,
    reduction = "pca",
    reduction.name = "tsne_rna",
    check_duplicates = FALSE,
    verbose = FALSE
  )
} else {
  log_msg("Rtsne not installed; skipping tSNE on RNA PCA.", log_file = log_file)
}

# 2) Harmony embeddings
if (requireNamespace("harmony", quietly = TRUE)) {
  seu_int <- withCallingHandlers(
    run_harmony_compat(seu_obj = seu_int, batch_col = batch_col, dims = 1:30),
    warning = function(w) {
      log_msg("Harmony warning: ", conditionMessage(w), log_file = log_file)
      invokeRestart("muffleWarning")
    }
  )

  seu_int <- RunUMAP(
    seu_int,
    dims = 1:30,
    reduction = "harmony",
    reduction.name = "umap_harmony",
    n.neighbors = 30,
    min.dist = 0.3,
    verbose = FALSE
  )

  if (requireNamespace("Rtsne", quietly = TRUE)) {
    seu_int <- RunTSNE(
      seu_int,
      dims = 1:30,
      reduction = "harmony",
      reduction.name = "tsne_harmony",
      check_duplicates = FALSE,
      verbose = FALSE
    )
  }

  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig16_Harmony_UMAP_cell_type.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", CFG$cols$cell_type, "Harmony UMAP by cell type"))
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig17_Harmony_UMAP_donor.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", batch_col, "Harmony UMAP by donor"))
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig18_Harmony_UMAP_infection.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", CFG$cols$infection, "Harmony UMAP by infection"))
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig19_Harmony_UMAP_stage.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", CFG$cols$stage, "Harmony UMAP by stage"))
  save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig20_Harmony_UMAP_condition.pdf"),
                   safe_dimplot(seu_int, "umap_harmony", "condition", "Harmony UMAP by condition"))

  if ("tsne_harmony" %in% names(seu_int@reductions)) {
    save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig21_Harmony_tSNE_cell_type.pdf"),
                     safe_dimplot(seu_int, "tsne_harmony", CFG$cols$cell_type, "Harmony tSNE by cell type"))
    save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig22_Harmony_tSNE_infection.pdf"),
                     safe_dimplot(seu_int, "tsne_harmony", CFG$cols$infection, "Harmony tSNE by infection"))
    save_if_not_null(file.path(CFG$dirs$figures, "Fig23_Harmony_tSNE_stage.pdf"),
                     safe_dimplot(seu_int, "tsne_harmony", CFG$cols$stage, "Harmony tSNE by stage"))
  }

  write_legend(
    "Fig16-23", "Integration sensitivity with Harmony + UMAP/tSNE",
    hypothesis = "Cross-donor comparability can improve after correction without erasing infection/time biology.",
    methods = "Run PCA, Harmony (donor batch), then UMAP and tSNE on Harmony embeddings; color by cell type, donor, infection, stage, and condition.",
    readout = "Desired: donor mixing improves while biological structure remains interpretable.",
    interpretation_template = "- If donor still dominates, revisit QC/batch definition.\n- If infection/stage structure vanishes, integration may be over-correcting.",
    outfile = file.path(CFG$dirs$legends, "Fig16_23_legend.md")
  )
} else {
  log_msg("Harmony not installed; skipping Harmony integration.", log_file = log_file)
}

qs::qsave(seu_int, file.path(CFG$dirs$objects, "seu_with_integration_checks.qs"))
log_msg("07_integration_sensitivity done.", log_file = log_file)
Why this is better

This version fixes all the major issues:

seu_int gets its own PCA before UMAP/Harmony

the full object is preserved

downsampling is only a fallback, not automatic data loss

duplicate preprocessing is removed

Harmony version mismatch stays handled

your downsampling is more representative and closer to the requested cell target

What I would do scientifically

For a Nature-level analysis, I would treat this as a sensitivity check, not the main integrated object.

Use:

full object for core biological conclusions whenever feasible

downsampled object only for rapid embedding diagnostics or Harmony tuning

Then compare:

full PCA/UMAP vs downsampled PCA/UMAP

cell-type proportions preserved?

donor mixing improved?

infection/stage separation preserved?

FIB2 position and trophoblast invasion axis stable?

If those are stable, the downsampled integration-check figure is defensible as a computational convenience rather than a biological shortcut.

One more thing about your memory issue

Because you are on Windows and had std::bad_alloc, a very practical approach is:

options(future.globals.maxSize = 8 * 1024^3)   # if using future anywhere
gc()

But the bigger win is simply not preprocessing the full object and the subset in the same script path.

Your old script was effectively doing expensive work on seu, then trying to analyze seu_int anyway.

Minimal fix if you want the smallest change possible

If you want to change as little as possible, replace this block:

seu_int <- downsample_for_speed(seu, max_cells = 120000, seed = 42)

seu <- ScaleData(seu, features = VariableFeatures(seu), verbose = FALSE)
seu <- RunPCA(seu, features = VariableFeatures(seu), npcs = 50, verbose = FALSE)

with this:

seu_int <- downsample_for_speed(seu, max_cells = 120000, seed = 42)
log_msg("Integration sensitivity running on ", ncol(seu_int), " cells (from ", ncol(seu), ").", log_file = log_file)

seu_int <- NormalizeData(seu_int, verbose = FALSE)
seu_int <- FindVariableFeatures(seu_int, nfeatures = 3000, verbose = FALSE)
seu_int <- ScaleData(seu_int, features = VariableFeatures(seu_int), verbose = FALSE)
seu_int <- RunPCA(seu_int, features = VariableFeatures(seu_int), npcs = 50, verbose = FALSE)

That alone will fix the pca not found crash.
